@keyframes spin {
  to {
    transform: rotate(360deg);
  }
}
@keyframes ping {
  75%, 100% {
    transform: scale(2);
    opacity: 0;
  }
}
@keyframes pulse {
  50% {
    opacity: 0.5;
  }
}
@keyframes bounce {
  0%, 100% {
    transform: translateY(-25%);
    animation-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0.8, 0, 1, 1);
  }
  50% {
    transform: none;
    animation-timing-function: cubic-bezier(0, 0, 0.2, 1);
  }
}
